කොට්ඨාශය” නමින්‌ මෙය හදුන්වන ලදි.

සේවා පුළුල්‌ කිරීමේ අරමුණන්‌ රත්මලාන ඩිපෝ පරිශ්‍රය තුළ පිහිටුවා තිබූ වෛද්‍ය

170 දරණ ස්ථානයට ගෙන එන ලද අතර, වර්තමානයේ “ජාතික ප්‍රවාහන වෛද්‍ය

1097 අංක 25 දරණ ජාතික ප්‍රවාහන වෛද්‍ය ආයතන පනත මගින්‌ ස්ථාපිත කර ඇත.

ප්‍රා දේශිකයේ ප්‍රධාන කළමණාකරුවෙත හා 2016.12.29, 2017.08.23 දිනැති ව ශ්‍රිලංකා ගමනා
ගමන මණ්ඩල සභාපතිතුමා වෙත ලිපි යොමු කළද මේ වන තෙක්‌ ප්‍රතිචාරයක්‌ දක්වා නැත.

2018 දෙසැම්බර්‌ 31 බනට ගෙවිය යුතු මුදලින්‌ 2018 වර්ෂයට හිමි ගමන්‌ අවසර පත්‍ර සඳහා රු.9,428,208.74
ක්‌ 2019 වර්ෂයේ ගෙවා ඇත. ඉදිරි මුදල්‌ ගෙවීම සඳහා කටයුතු කරනු ලැබේ.

26


2018 වර්ෂයේ කාර්ය සාධනය ඉහළ නැංවීම සඳහා අනුගමනය කල කියා මාර්ග.

ක ජනපති නිල මෙහෙවර යටත්‌ කුරුණැගල හා වවුනියාව දිස්ත්‍රික්යේ ජංගම සේවාවන්‌ පැවැත්වීම.

ක ගාඛා කාර්යාල 25 න්‌ මහනුවර, ගාල්ල, කුරුණැගල, අනුරාධපුරය, හම්බන්තාට, බදුල්ල, අම්පාර,
මඞඩකලපුව, වේරහැර, මාතර, වවුනියාව, මන්නාරම, ත්‍රිකුණාමලය, කිලිනොච්චිය, යාපනය, ගම්පහ,
කළුතර, මුලතිව්‌ සහ පුත්තලම යන ශාඛා වල පරිගණක ජාලගත කිරීම අවසන්‌ කිරීම.

ක මන්නාරම දිස්ත්‍රික්‌ කාර්යාලය සඳහා මන්නාරම දස්ත්‍රික්‌ ලේකම්‌ කාර්යාලටය අයිති ගොඩනැගිල්ලක
පළමු මහලේ ඉඩකඩ වෙන්‌ කර එහි නවීකරණ කටයුතු සිදු කිරීම.

2018.12.31 දනට මුදල්‌ ප්‍රවාහ ප්‍රකාශය

මෙහෙයුම්‌ කටයුතුවලින්‌ ලද මුදල්‌ පුවාහය
සාමාන්‍ය මෙහෙයුම්‌ අතිරික්තය

ක්ෂය ගැලපීම්‌

පාරිතෝෂික වෙන්කිරීම

ආයෝජන පොළී

කාරක ප්‍රාග්ධන වෙනස්වීම්‌ වලට පෙර මෙහෙයුම්‌ ලාභය

නොග වැසි වීම

ලැබිය යුතු ගිණුම්‌ වැඩි ටීම

අනිකුත්‌ ලැබීම්‌ වැඩි වීම

ගෙවිය යුතු ගිණුම්‌ වැඩි වීම

උපචිත වියදම්‌ වැඩිවීම

අනිකුත්‌ වියදම්‌ වැඩි වීම

විශ්වාෂ රක්ෂණ ඇප තැන්පතු වැඩිවීම
ක්ෂය වෙන්‌ කිරීම්‌ ගැළපීම

පෙර වෂර්යේ ගැළපීම්‌

මෙහෙයුම්‌ කටයුතුවලින්‌ ජනිත වූ මුදල්‌ පුචාහය
පාරිතෝෂික ගෙවීම්‌

භාණ්ඩාගාර ඒකාබද්ධ අරමුදලට දායකත්වය

මෙහෙයුම්‌ කටයුතුවල ශුද්ධ මුදල්‌ පූවාහය

ආයෝජන ක්‍රියාකාරකම්‌ වලින්‌ ලද මුදල්‌ පුවාහය

ස්ථාවර වත්කම්‌ මිලට ගැනීම

නොනිමි වැඩ — ඉදිකිරීම්‌

ආයෝජන මිලදී ගැනීම්‌ ( ශුද්ධ)
ආයෝජන පොළී

විකුණුම්‌ ක්‍රියාකාරිත්වය - වත්කම්‌ විකුණුම්‌

ආයෝජන ක්‍රියාකාරකම්‌ වලින්‌ ලද ශුද්ධ මුදල්‌ ප්‍රවාහය

ඉද්ධ වැඩි වීම මුදල්‌ හා බැංකු ශේෂය
ආරම්භක ශේෂය මුදල්‌ හා බැංකු

අවසාන ශේෂය මුදල්‌ හා බැංකු

මූල්‍ය ප්‍රකාශනයේ පිටු අංක 32 සිට 42 දක්වා ගිණුම්කරණ ප්‍රතිපත්ති සහ සටහන්‌ අන්තගර්ත වේ.

31


ජාතික ප්‍රවාහන වෛඳ්‍ය ආයතනය
මූල්‍ය ප්‍රකාශන පිළිබඳ සටහන්‌
2017 දෙසැම්බර්‌ 31 ඉන අවසන්‌ වන වර්ෂය

1. සංයුක්ත තොරතුරු

Ll    සාමාන්‍ය

ජාතික ප්‍රවාහන වෛද්‍ය ආයතනය, ඨී ලංකා ප්‍රජාතාන්ත්‍රික සමාජවාදී ජනරජයේ 1007 අංක 25 දරන
ජාතික ප්‍රවාහන වෛද්‍ය ආයතන පනත මගින්‌ ස්ථාපනය කරනු ලැබිය. මෙහි ලියාපදිංචි කාර්යාලය
නුගේගොඩ, හයිලෙවල්‌ පාරේ අංක 170 දරණ ස්ථානයේ පිහිටා ඇත.

ආයතනය එහි සේවාවන්‌ දිවයින පුරාම පුළුල්කර ආයතනය එක්‌ දිස්ත්‍රික්කයක්‌ සඳහා එක්‌ ශාඛාවක්‌
ස්ථාපනය කිරීමට හා එමගින්‌ ප්‍රධාන කාර්යාලය හැර ශාඛා කාර්යාල 25 මගින්‌ මුළු අවයිනම ආවරණය
කිරීම සඳහා ප්‍රතිපත්තිමය තීරණයක්‌ ගෙන ඇත.

1.2 මූලික කාර්යයන්‌ හා මෙහෙයුම්‌ ස්වභාවය

ආයතනයේ දැක්ම වන්නේ ජාතියට ප්‍රවාහන වෛද්‍ය පහසුකම්‌ ලබාදීමයි. මෙම දැක්ම ලඟාකර ගැනීමේ
මූලික පියවර ලෙස ජාතික ප්‍රවාහන වෛද්‍ය ආයතනය ඊයදුරු අයදුම්කරුවන්‌ සඳහා බඳවා ගැනීම්වලදී
හා කලින්‌ කලට වෛද්‍ය පහසුකම්‌ සලසා දෙනු ලැබේ.

මීට අමතරව උසාවි මගින්‌ හා ප්‍රවාහන පොලිසිය මගින්‌ යොමූ කරන ලද රියදුරන්‌ සඳහා වෛද්‍ය
පරික්ෂණ සිදුකිරීම හා උසාවියට වෛද්‍ය වාර්තා ඉදිරිපත්‌ කිරීම සිදු කෙරේ. ජාතික ප්‍රවාහන වෛද්‍ය
ආයතනය මගින්‌ පෞද්ගලික බස්රථ රියදුරන්ට මාර්ග බලපත්‍ර ලබාගැනීම සඳහා අවශ්‍ය වෛද්‍ය
යෝග්‍යතා සහතික ලබාදෙන අතර රාජ්‍ය හා පෞද්ගලික අංශයේ ආයතන මගින්‌ අයදුම්‌ කරන ඊයදාරන්‌
සඳහා වෛද්‍ය යෝග්‍යතාවය සහතික කිරීමද සිදුකෙරේ. ආයතනය මගින්‌ රී.ලං.ග.ම සේවකයන්‌ සඳහා
රැකියා පූර්ව වෛද්‍ය පරික්ෂණ සිදුකරනු ලබයි.

එමගින්‌ රී.ලං.ග.ම හා ජර්මන්‌ කාර්මික විද්‍යාලයේ සේවකයන්‌ සඳහා බාහිර රෝගී ප්‍රතිකාර ඒකකයක්‌ ද
පවත්වාගෙන යනු ලැබේ.

2.    අනුකලතා ප්‍රකාශය
ආයතනයේ මූල්‍ය ප්‍රකාශන රී ලංකා රාජ්‍ය අංශ ගිණුම්කරණ ප්‍රමිතීන්ට අනුකලව පිළියෙල කර තිබේ.
2.1 පිළියෙල කිරීමේ පඳනම

ආයතනයේ මූල්‍ය ප්‍රකාශන පැරණ පිරිවැය පදනම මත පිළියෙල කර ඇත. මූල්‍ය ප්‍රකාශන පිළියෙල
කිරීම හා ඉදිරිපත්‌ කිරීම ශී ලංකා රාජ්‍ය අංශ ගිණුම්කරණ පුමිති අංක 01 ට අනුකලවේ.
මූල්‍ය ප්‍රකාශන ශී ලංකා රුපියල්‌ (රු.) වලින්‌ ඉදිරිපත්‌ කර ඇත.

32


ජාතික ප්‍රචාහන වෛද්‍ය ආයතනය
මූල්‍ය ප්‍රකාශය පිළිබඳ සටහන්‌
2018 දෙසැම්බර්‌ 31 දින අවසන්‌ වචන වෂර්ය

3. සුවිශේෂී ගිණුම්‌ ප්‍රතිපත්ති පිළිබඳ සාරාංශය

3.1 දේපළ, පිරියත හා උපකරණ

දෝපළ, පිරියත හා උපකරණ මූලික වශයෙන්‌ පිරිවැයක්‌ ලෙස දක්වා ඇත. දරන ලද වියදම්‌ දේපල,
පිරියත හා උපකරණවල ධාරිතාව හා පැවැත්ම ඉහල නැංවීම සඳහා අදාල වන්නේ නම්‌ එම වියදම්‌
දෝපළ පිරියත හා උපකරණ සදහා වන පිරිවැයක්‌ ලෙස සැලකේ. වෙනත්‌ සියළු අළුත්වැඩියාවන්‌ හා
නඩත්තු වියදම්‌ ලාභ හං පාඩු ලෙස හඳුනාගෙන ඇත.

වත්කම්වල ප්‍රයෝජනවත්‌ ආයුකාලය සලකා සෘජු රේඛා පදනම මත ක්ෂයවීම ගණනය කිරීම පහත
දක්වා ඇත.

ගොඩනැගිලි                      -        අවූ. 40
යන්ත්‍රෝපකරණ             -      අවු. 10
ගෘහ භාණ්ඩ හා උපාංග          -        අවු. 10
වාහන                         -       අවූ. 5

වෛද්‍ය උපකරණ             -       අවූ. 10
තාප්ප බිත්ති                     -        අවූ. 40
පරිඝනක උපකරණ             -        අවු. 4

දෝපල, යන්ත්‍රෝපකරණ හා උපකරණ මිලට ගත්‌ වසරේසිට ක්ෂයවේ.

3.2 බඩු වට්ටෝරු ලේඛන
බඩු වට්ටෝරු පිරිවැය අනුව ගණනය කෙරේ.

3.3 පාරිතෝෂික ප්‍රතිලාභ

අදාල ප්‍රඥාප්තිය අනුව ආයතනය පාරිතෝෂික ගෙවීම සදහා වගකිව යුතුය. ජාතික ප්‍රවාහන වෛද්‍ය
ආයතනය ඇතිකරන අවස්ථාවේදී ශ්‍රී.ලං.ග.ම සිට එය වෙත මාරු කරන ලද සේවකයන්‌ සදහා මෙම
විශේෂ ප්‍රතිලාභ ලබාගැනීම සඳහා විශේෂ විධිවිධාන සලසා ඇත. මෙම ටිශේෂ ටවියිටිධාන සඳහා
අධ්‍යක්ෂ මණ්ඩලයේ තීරණය ලබාගෙන තිබේ. මෙම තත්වයන්‌ දෙක පදනම්‌ කරගෙන එක්‌ එක්‌
වසර සඳහා ප්‍රතිපාදන සලසනු ලැබේ.

353


34

ජාතික ප්‍රවාහන වෛද්‍ය ආයතනය

වෛද්‍ය සැපයුම්‌

වෛද්‍ය උපකරණ නඩත්තුව

පවිත්‍රතා ගාස්තු

විගණන ගාස්තු වෙන්‌ කිරීම

වෛද්‍ය රක්ෂණය

නිල ඇඳුම්‌ හා නිල හැදුනුම්පත්‌

ගොඩනැගලි කුලී

පෞද්ගලික ආරක්ෂක ගාස්තු

ගෙවිය යුතු විදුලිය

ගෙවිය යුතු දුරකතන

ගෙවිය යුතු ජලය

ගෙවිය යුතු පානීය ජලය

ගෙවිය යුතු බැංකු ණය වාරික

ගෙවිය යුතු මහජන බැංකු ණය වාරික

ගෙවිය යුතු සණස බැංකු ණය වාරික

ගෙවිය යුතු රුහුණු සංවධර්න බැංකු ණය වාරික
ගෙවිය යුතු නිවාස සංවධර්න බැංකු ණය වාරික
ගෙවිය යුතු ප්‍රාදෝශීය සංවධර්න බැංකු ණය වාරික
ගෙවිය යුතු කායර්සාධන ඇපකර

ගෙවිය යුතු ප්‍රතිපුරණ රක්ෂණ

ගෙවිය යුතු වෙනන්‌ වියදම්‌

වෙනත්‌ ගෙවිය යුතු

වේතන පාලන ගිණුම්‌

කාල පදනම මත හා වෙනන්‌ ගෙවිය යුතු වේතන
ඉදිරියට ගෙනා වැටුප්‌ ශේෂ

වෛද්‍ය කඳවූරු සහ වත්කම්‌ සමීක්ෂණ දීමනා
ගෙවිය යුතු පූහුණු දීමනා

ගෙවිය යුතු ගමන්‌ වියදම්‌

National Transport Medical Institute

Introduction

The institute had primarily been established as a medical centre owned by South-
Western Bus Company in Ratmalana depot premises which provided medical
facilities to the employees of the Company. With the nationalization of Bus
Companies in 1058, the ownership of the medical centre was vested upon the
National Transport Board and was thereafter renamed as ““C.T.B. Medical

Division”.

With the aim of extending its services the medical centre in Ratmalana was shifted
to No. 170, High level Road, Nugegoda in 1070 and is currently functioning under
the name of “National Transport Medical Institute” as a Self income generating

institution under Ministry of Transport as a Government Statutory Institution.

This institution has been established by the National Transport Medical Institute
act No. 25 of 1007. In order to attain the main objective of the institute it has
extended its services further, through the establishment of twenty five (25) branch
offices including the Head office throughout the Island.

Although it has been only 10 years since the commencement of NTMIL its

contribution towards the nation has always been gigantic.

National Transport Medical Institute


Vision

"Placing a healthy driver behind cach steering wheel"

Mission

"To be the leader in the transport medical ficld and to issue medical certificates after a qualitative
medical examination to ensure the physical and mental condition of all driver applicants"

Objectives

Examine physical and mental fitness of all the candidates applying for diving licences.
Improve the quality and security stratagem of the medical certificate issued to candidates.
Achieve quality of the service through effective human resources management.

Functions of the Institute

(@

(b)

(©)

(d

(©

(D

@

To provide medical services to drivers and operators of all types of vehicles including
heavy vehicles.

To examine physical and mental fitness of drivers of all types of vehicles including heavy
vehicles and issue certificates to them.

To conduct medical examinations for drivers and operators of all types of vehicles and
make recommendations regarding their fitness and suitability.

To provide necessary medical services and assistance in cases of road accidents relating to
any type of motor vehicles.

To ensure that all types of motor vehicles are driven or operated only by persons
physically and mentally fit and competent, by the institution itself or in consultation with
other organizations.

To provide medical advices and recommendations on industrial hygiene and industrial
accidents.

To formulate standards and prescribe parameters pertaining to transport medical activities

to be adopted by the relevant implementing authorities.

Opinion

The audit of the financial statements of the National Transport Medical Institute for the year
ended 31 December 2018 comprising the statement of financial position as at 31 December
2018 and the statement of financial performance, statement of changes in equity and cash
flow Statement for the year then ended, and notes to the financial statements, including a
Summary of significant accounting policies, was carried out under my direction in pursuance
of provisions in Article 154(1) of the Constitution of the Democratic Socialist Republic of Sri
Lanka read in conjunction with provisions of the National Audit Act No. 19 of 2018 and the
Finance Act No.3$8 of 1071. My report to Parliament in pursuance of provisions in Article 154
(0) of the Constitution will be tabled in due course.

In my opinion, the financial statements give a true and fair view of the financial position of
the National Transport Medical Instituteas at 31 December 2018, and of its financial
performance and cash flows for the year then ended in accordance with Sri Lanka Public

Sector Accounting Standards.

Basis for Opinion

I conducted my audit in accordance with Sri Lanka Auditing Standards (SLAUuSS). My
responsibilitics, under those standards are further described in the Auditor’s Responsibilitics
for the Audit of the Financial Statementssection of my report. 1 believe that the audit
evidence 1 have obtained is sufficient and appropriate to provide a basis for myqualificd

opinion.

Responsibilities of Management and Those Charged with Governance for the Financial

Statements

Management is responsible for the preparation of financial statements that give a truce and fair
view in accordance with Sri Lanka Public Sector Accounting Standards and for such internal
control as management determine is necessary to enable the preparation of financial

Statements that are free from material misstatement, whether due to fraud or error.

In preparing the financial statements, management is responsible for assessing the Medical
Institute’s ability to continue as a going concern, disclosing, as applicable, matters related to
going concern and using the going concern basis of accounting unless management cither
intend to liquidate the Medical Institute or to cease operations, or has no realistic alternative

but to do so.

Those charged with governance are responsible for oversceing the Medical Institute’s
financial reporting process.

As per Sub-section 16(1) of the National Audit Act No. 19 of 2018, the Institute is required to
maintain proper books and records of all its income, expenditure, assets and liabilitics, to

enable annual and periodic financial statements to be prepared.

Auditor’s Responsibilities for the Audit of the Financial Statements

My objective is to obtain reasonable assurance about whether the financial statements as a
whole arc free from material misstatement, whether duc to fraud or crror, and to issuc an
auditor’s report that includes my opinion. Reasonable assurance is a high level of assurance,
but is not a guarantee that an audit conducted in accordance with Sri Lanka Auditing
Standards will always detect a material misstatement when it exists. Misstatements can arise
from fraud or error and are considered material if, individually or in the aggregate, they could
reasonably be expected to influence the economic decisions of users taken on the basis of

these financial statements.

As part of an audit in accordance with Sri Lanka Auditing Standards, I exercise professional

Judgment and maintain professional scepticism throughout the audit. I also:

e Identify and assess the risks of material misstatement of the financial statements, whether
due to fraud or error, design and perform audit procedures responsive to those risks, and
obtain audit evidence that is sufficient and appropriate to provide a basis for my opinion.
The risk of not detecting a material misstatement resulting from fraud is higher than for
one resulting from crror, as fraud may involve collusion, forgery, intentional omissions,

misrepresentations, or the override of internal control.

e Obtain an understanding of internal control relevant to the Institute in order to design audit
procedures that are appropriate in the circumstances, but not for the purpose of expressing

an opinion on the effectiveness of the Institute’s internal control.

(Dh       For the construction works of the 02" stage relating to renovation of the building , the
contract worth Rs.43,023,6041 had been awarded to the above contractor without
calling for bids on the basis of completion of the contract by 21 January 2010, but the
agreed works had not been completed even by 30 April 2010. Nevertheless,
liquidated damages had not been recovered from the contractor in terms of the
agreements. In making payments for the completed works of the contract, a sum of
Rs.8307,848 had been overpaid to the contractor together with the VAT. Similarly, 4
items the estimated cost of which was Rs. 1,448,776 had not been completed with the
usc of building materials in prescribed specification as agreed by the agreement and

consultant approval too had not been obtained thereon.

(Cc)     Expenditure of Rs.4,630,631 had been incurred for the renovation activities of the
Second floor of the Institute before the year 2017. Anew contract agreement had bcen
entered into for the building renovation activities and a sum of Rs.406,348,205 had
been spent thereon in the year 2017. Accordingly, the total sum of Rs.4,630,631

Spent before the year 2017 had become a fruitless cxpenditure.

(dq)    According to the Action Plan 2018, the Institute had planned to construct two
buildings for the Anuradhapura and Kandy branches. Since necessary approval had
not been obtained, Constructions of the buildings on those lands had not been
commenced cven by April 2010. As such, these offices are maintained in the rented
buildings at present and a sum of Rs.006,875 and Rs.1,006,500 had been paid as

rentals respectively for the Anuradhapura branch and Kandy branch during the year.

03.        Other Audit Observations

(a)        The Institute had not taken action to prepare Action Plan to suit to the objectives.

(bh      Even though the Department of Management Services had approved 454 staff for 33
posts of the Institute on 23 November 2017 and 15 May 2018, recruitments for 10
key posts of the Institute had not been made even by February 201°. Similarly, oO
medical officers on permanent basis and 28 medical officers on contract basis had
been employed by the Institute as at 31 December 2018. Accordingly, 34 posts of
Medical Officers had fallen vacant,but necessary steps had not been taken to fill those

vacancies.

(0)       It was observed at the audit test check carricd out on the National Transport Medical
Institute that out of the Medical Officers who had been recruited on the basis of
hourly wages, 11 officers had not reported to the service by 31 December 2018 and
action had not been taken so as to prevent them from issuing medical certificates by
informing the Commissioner of Motor Traffic on such medical officers who had not

reported to the Service.

(dD       It was observed that out of the accounts balance of Rs. 14,700,018 receivable as at 31
December 2018, a balance of Rs.9,061,037 was older than 650 days and it
represented 07.72 per cent of the total receivable balance. Similarly, a sum of
Rs. 742,312 had remained unrecovered from a private bus company for over 03 years
as at 31 December 2018 , whereas action had not been taken to recover those monies.
Further, out of Rs.33,588,765 payable by the Institute as at 31 December 2018, a sum
of Rs.6,000,722 or 21 per cent remained unsettled for over a period of 650 days.

02.         Report on other legal and regulatory requirements

(a) IT would like to mention that appropriate steps have been taken to systematically
dispose of hemorrhagic spines and cotton wool used in the laboratory. It is duc to be
looked for a place to accept those wastes and to take steps accordingly. Enquiries in
this connection have been made from the Government institutions.

(bh) It has been submitted to the Ministry of Finance for approval, but no response has
been received up to date. However, steps have been taken to invest the moncy in
fixed deposits and treasury bills for the nceds of the institution as well as to credit to

the Consolidated Account of the General Treasury.

(c) The board of survey activities for the year 2018 has been completed by now. That

report is due to be submitted to the relevant sections.

(d) This allowance is paid as an incentive to the staff with the approval of the Board of
Directors. With a limited staff, services arc provided approximately to 4500 clients
per day and Services at several branch offices including the Head Office are
commenced between 7.00 am and 7.30 am. This allowance is paid as an incentive for
the them as they are committed to serving the public and the institution while
Sacrificing their personal needs. I would like to mention that the National Transport
Medical Institute is the only government institution to start providing the service to
the public from 7.00 am.

Likely, although all the employees of the Institute are entitled to 42 days leave per
year, as 1t is difficult to continue the activities of the Institute when they intend to get
that privilege at their will, the attendance allowance is paid with the aim of

maintaining a good level of staff attendance and minimizing the chances of late

The Public Administration Circular No. 35/2017 dated 26 December 2017 has been
issued to Government Institutions and Officers and our Institute is a semi government
institute functioning under the control of the Ministry of Transport and Civil

Aviation.

Under the Board Decisions No. 2015/56 taken on 18.11.2015 this has been approved
as book loans.This special advance is provided by our Institute as a loan to the
employees. Out of this loan amount of Rs.25000.00, advance amount of Rs.4000.00 1s
deducted and 4.2% interest is charged on the remaining amount. Action has been
taken to recover the loan within 10 months.

Public Administration Circular No. 07/2017 dated 26th March 2015 has been issued
for public institutions and officials and our institute is a Semi government institute
functioning under the control of the Ministry of Transport and Civil Aviation. .AS per
the Board Decision No. 2016/07 of the Board of Directors meeting held on
30.06.2016, approval has been received to pay Rs. 15,000.00 as festival advance and
Rs. 15,000.00 as an advance to purchase cloth. Action has been taken to recover the

advances within 10 months.

It has been specified by the circulars No.SB / 02/01 dated 25 September 2015 issued
by the Secretary to the President that the ceremonies to be held for projects
implemented on foreign aid / loans, conferences and workshops should not be held in
high-end luxury hotels at high cost.

Also, we have not held any event on 24 December 2018 and arrangements were made
to conduct the employees get together at the Topaz Hotel, Kandy on 2° December
2018. Since that occasion was not a Ceremony, conference or workshop, held for

foreign aid / loan based projects as mentioned in the Secretary to the President's


Circular No. SB / 02/01, it is hereby stated that this was not done contrary to the Said

Circular.

National Transport Medical Institute

NOTES TO THE FINANCIAL STATEMENTS

1.2

Corporate Information

General

National Transport Medical Institute was established in terms of the National Transport Medical
Institute Act No 25 of 1997 of the government of the Democratic Socialist Republic of Sri Lanka.
The registered office of the Institute is located at No 170, High Level Road, Nugegoda.

The Institute expanded its services through out the island and established 25 branch per district
and covered whole island. Our Institute has an monopoly to conduct medical test to the drivers.

Our Vision is a healthy driver behind each steering.

Our Mission is " certify physical and mental fitness, conducting qualitative medical tests
for all the candidates applied for driving licenses.

Principal Activities and Nature of Operations

The vision of the organization is to provide transport medical care to the nation. As a preliminary
Step to achieve the vision, National Transport Medical Institute performs a medical examination
on driver applicants at the recruitment and periodically.

In addition to that medically assess the drivers who are being referred by courts and by the traffic
police and submit medical reports to courts. National Transport Medical Institute also provide
medical fitness certificates for private bus drivers when obtaining their route permit and certify
medical fitness of drivers applying from government and private sector organizations. The
organization performs a pre employment medical assessment of employees of SLTB.

It also provides an out door patient's treatment unit for employees of SLTB and Germen Technical
school.

Statement of Compliance

The Financial Statements of the Institute have been prepared in accordance with Sri Lanka Public
Sector Accounting Standards.

Basis of Preparation

The Financial Statements of the Institute have been prepared on a historical cost basis. The
preparation and presentation of the Financial Statements are in compliance with the Sri Lanka
Public Sector Accounting Standards No 1.

The Financial Statements are presented in Sri Lankan Rupees (LKR).

Summary of Significant Accounting Policies

Property Plant and Equipment

Property Plant and Equipment is initially stated at cost. If the Cost incurred are related with the
improvement of the capacity of Property Plant & Equipment and life time of the Property Plant &
Equipment which are recognized as cost of Property Plant & Equipment. All other repair and
maintenance costs are recognized in the profit and loss incurred.

Depreciation is calculated on a straight line basis over the useful life of assets as follows;

Building                       -          40 Years
Machinery                    -           10 Years
Furniture & Fittings              -             10 Years
Vehicle                       -           b Years
Medical Equipment             -           10 Years
Parapet Wall                    -            40 Years
Computer Equipment           -             a Years

Property Plant and Equipment are depreciated from the date of purchased.

Inventories

The inventories are valued at cost.

Benefit of Gratuity

The Institute is liable to pay gratuity in terms of the relevant statute. Special provisions are made
for the employees who were transferred from CTB to National Transport Medical Institute at the
Stage of formation of National Transport Medical Institute. Board decisions are obtained for these
Special provisions. Based on the both situations the provisions are made in the each year.
